份		꜂fan	陰上			A portion, a dividend, a share… A vulgar character. An old form of 彬 [꜀pan]. The proper sound in colloquial is [fan꜅], though sometimes read [꜂fan]. It is the same word as 分 [fan꜅] when used as a noun.
